Fruits become ripen and the insect will eat the contents int the fruit.For the traps put Methyl eugenol 5 ml + malathion 5 ml in water bottle or in a cover. make 3-4 holes and place them in the field at least 10-12.The chemical prepared with 5 grams of dried fish powder along with 1 ml Dichlorovos  can also be used as a bait.For every 20 days the chemical should be changed. these traps should be placed before the flowering season.\nFor the Nutrient deficiency spray multiplex 2 ml .

 \tFor the control of the fruit fly install Methyl Eugenol traps . Fruits become ripen and the insect will eat the contents int the fruit.For the traps put Methyl eugenol 5 ml + malathion 5 ml in water bottle or in a cover. make 3-4 holes and place them in the field at least 10-12.The chemical prepared with 5 grams of dried fish powder along with 1 ml Dichlorovos can also be used as a bait.For every 20 days the chemical should be changed. these traps should be placed before the flowering season.  \tFor the control of the fruit fly install Methyl Eugenol traps . Fruits become ripen and the insect will eat the contents int the fruit.For the traps put Methyl eugenol 5 ml + malathion 5 ml in water bottle or in a cover. make 3-4 holes and place them in the field at least 10-12.The chemical prepared with 5 grams of dried fish powder along with 1 ml Dichlorovos can also be used as a bait.For every 20 days the chemical should be changed. these traps should be placed before the flowering season.  \tFor the control of the fruit fly install Methyl Eugenol traps . Fruits become ripen and the insect will eat the contents int the fruit.For the traps put Methyl eugenol 5 ml + malathion 5 ml in water bottle or in a cover. make 3-4 holes and place them in the field at least 10-12.The chemical prepared with 5 grams of dried fish powder along with 1 ml Dichlorovos can also be used as a bait.For every 20 days the chemical should be changed. these traps should be placed before the flowering season.  \tFor the control of the fruit fly install Methyl Eugenol traps . Fruits become ripen and the insect will eat the contents int the fruit.For the traps put Methyl eugenol 5 ml + malathion 5 ml in water bottle or in a cover. make 3-4 holes and place them in the field at least 10-12.The chemical prepared with 5 grams of dried fish powder along with 1 ml Dichlorovos can also be used as a bait.For every 20 days the chemical should be changed. these traps should be placed before the flowering season.
